font-size: 11pt; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Eric Mill, Shweta Panditrao, Chrome Security Team</span></div>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Wed, 12 Aug 2020 17:29:00 +0000","feedId":649,"bgimg":"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/19onWpGRt7-kVhtL1k2vPaRCNh0fYDrGxT8bq8sT0rIiAMlAZyW_Ckzjsfv1TD92Yxr5iocJPPh5U3XJI5T9RJsVu44lhW3qwgff8hm13pZ7TgYCnTBlgUwgTQHqH9fGYSCakXoPMg","linkMd5":"fbbf8102a4045dd06f46fd70172284bf","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn17@2020_1/2020/08/16/12-29-50-568_3aca63f11d9df57d.webp","destWidth":592,"destHeight":254,"author":"Chromium Blog","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/19onWpGRt7-kVhtL1k2vPaRCNh0fYDrGxT8bq8sT0rIiAMlAZyW_Ckzjsfv1TD92Yxr5iocJPPh5U3XJI5T9RJsVu44lhW3qwgff8hm13pZ7TgYCnTBlgUwgTQHqH9fGYSCakXoPMg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn94@2020_5/2020/08/16/12-29-51-491_3aca63f11d9df57d.webp","https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/QDXiDdJ-BiNqDlHafhxg3XAUEsQOeHXOe6rm15aEkjp2kC1FIzvZp_yvTGG6tM0yCmYtDy74OYRTrDvfE3TnBtaM-GNwEpUB_FuTLEJLbOyQZjyAra3CbHBbBcB-6PY7DtNq0HQ0vg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn14@2020_2/2020/08/16/12-29-50-215_16dfc5e2c7e99e48.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-16 20:29:49","updatedTime":"2020-08-16 20:29:49","title":"Improving Chromium's browser compatibility in 2020","link":"http://blog.chromium.org/2020/06/improving-chromiums-browser.html","description":"<span id=\"docs-internal-guid-106a7249-7fff-d6e0-cae6-36f32a1a0bf8\"><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Last year, MDN ran the </span><a href=\"https://insights.developer.mozilla.org/\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">2019 Web Developer Needs Assessment (DNA) survey</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">. The DNA survey drew responses from over 28,000 developers from around the world, together contributing more than 10,000 hours of insights into what is and isn't working on the web today, and how the web needs to change to meet the needs of the developer community.</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">There were many needs expressed in the </span><a href=\"https://mdn-web-dna.s3-us-west-2.amazonaws.com/MDN-Web-DNA-Report-2019.pdf\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">survey results</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">, but one that stood out clearly was </span><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">browser compatibility</span><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> - the manner in which websites look or behave differently on different web browsers. It is clear that it is still painful to develop a website or web app that works reliably across browsers.</span></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"><br /></span></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"></span></p>\n <table align=\"center\" cellpadding=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\" class=\"tr-caption-container\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\">\n  <tbody>\n   <tr>\n    <td style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8TebBC73ZJI/Xuyhb3lkHkI/AAAAAAAABN8/aa0ROlMNtXgxAE5BOeGuUg4PjBc7qkYpwCK4BGAsYHg/s902/Screenshot%2B2020-05-15%2Bat%2B09.23.59.jpg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"277\" data-original-width=\"902\" height=\"193\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8TebBC73ZJI/Xuyhb3lkHkI/AAAAAAAABN8/aa0ROlMNtXgxAE5BOeGuUg4PjBc7qkYpwCK4BGAsYHg/w625-h193/Screenshot%2B2020-05-15%2Bat%2B09.23.59.jpg\" width=\"625\" /></a></td>\n   </tr>\n   <tr>\n    <td class=\"tr-caption\" style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 9pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">The div that looks different in every browser' (</span><a href=\"https://twitter.com/Martijn_Cuppens/status/1015169981368225793\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 9pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">credit Martijn Cuppens</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 9pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">) - it still reproduces today!</span></td>\n   </tr>\n  </tbody>\n </table><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">To help focus in on specific developer needs, MDN ran a follow-up survey in March 2020 - the MDN Browser Compatibility Survey. This survey, taken by over 3000 web developers and augmented by post-survey interviews, aimed to uncover the specific pain-points the web developer community is having with browser compatibility. Today I'd like to talk about our takeaways from the results, and what we - Google Chrome - are doing about them.</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">It is important to stress that these are just some early findings from the MDN Browser Compatibility survey and are focused on pain points developers have relating to Chrome.</span></p><h2 dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 6pt; margin-top: 18pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 16pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Flexbox</span></h2><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><a href=\"https://web.dev/responsive-web-design-basics/#flexbox\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Flexbox</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> is a powerful tool for layout on the web. It offers an ergonomic way to define layouts that will respond gracefully on different sized viewports. But this power isn't much good when it can't be relied on across browsers. Flexbox is one of our top priorities for browser compatibility across the web in 2020, and we've put heavy investment into it already.</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">The Chrome rendering team has been working on a rearchitecture of the Chromium flexbox implementation on top of our modern </span><a href=\"https://www.chromium.org/blink/layoutng\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">LayoutNG layout engine</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">. This work, which we plan to bring to Chrome 84, is expected to fix a number of Flexbox compatibility issues in Chromium.</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">We're also working towards bringing</span><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> </span><a href=\"https://crbug.com/762679\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">flex-gap</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> and </span><a href=\"http://crbug.com/375693\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">fieldset+flex</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> support to Chromium </span><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">this year. In fact, flex-gap will be available in Chrome 84 - try it out and </span><a href=\"https://twitter.com/ChromiumDev\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">let us know</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> what you think.</span></p><h2 dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 6pt; margin-top: 18pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 16pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Scrolling</span></h2><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Getting scrolling right in one browser can be tricky. Getting scrolling right across multiple browsers can be painful (for example, it takes </span><a href=\"https://github.com/willmcpo/body-scroll-lock\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">an entire library</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> to consistently lock body scrolling). We're still digging through the feedback on scrolling compatibility, but a few key areas have stood out so far:</span></p><br />\n <ul style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n  <li dir=\"ltr\" style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\"><p dir=\"ltr\" role=\"presentation\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">How virtual keyboards affect - or don't affect - viewport units in different browsers. (Note recent work from Microsoft Edge on a </span><a href=\"https://groups.google.com/a/chromium.org/d/msg/blink-dev/q80uCrMgiTM/nF3mo-7zBAAJ\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">VirtualKeyboard API</span></a><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> that may help here.)</span></p></li>\n  <li dir=\"ltr\" style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\"><p dir=\"ltr\" role=\"presentation\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">A lack of consistency in input-related events, and the outcome of interacting with them (e.g. what happens when you </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;roboto mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">preventDefault()</span><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> a </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;roboto mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">touchmove</span><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">).</span></p></li>\n  <li dir=\"ltr\" style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\"><p dir=\"ltr\" role=\"presentation\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Difficulty controlling how scrolling behaves across browsers (e.g. via scroll anchoring).</span></p></li>\n </ul><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">We plan to start here by investing more in understanding how we can effectively improve scrolling on the web. As part of that, we need to keep hearing from you. </span><a href=\"http://blog.chromium.org/2020/06/improving-chromiums-browser.html#summing-up\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Please continue to tell us about your scrolling compatibility pains</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> - especially as they relate to Chrome.</span></p><h2 dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 6pt; margin-top: 18pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 16pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Form controls</span></h2><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Forms are a very old part of the web, added before even CSS. Form controls were intended to mimic the look and feel of the native platform, but it's clear that they have failed to do so consistently and have also failed to keep up with the needs of modern web development. The compatibility survey turned up two general themes here: stylability and inconsistent behavior across browsers.</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">On styling form controls, the Microsoft Edge and Google Chrome teams recently finished </span><a href=\"https://blog.chromium.org/2020/03/updates-to-form-controls-and-focus.html\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">a year-long project to refresh and update the default form styles in Chromium-based browsers</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">. This much needed refresh modernizes the default look and brings improved accessibility and touch support. However it's clear that without more control over how form controls are styled, they still present a compatibility pain for web developers. We don't have anything to announce here today, but we will be continuing to look at form stylability during 2020.</span></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"><br /></span></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"></p>\n <table align=\"center\" cellpadding=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\" class=\"tr-caption-container\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\">\n  <tbody>\n   <tr>\n    <td style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ZkvwVqhZu00/Xuyh83uAZ6I/AAAAAAAABOQ/veJ_KXh8mFEB2uxPp_H82FwdQlTVlN6bgCK4BGAsYHg/s1600/Screenshot%2B2020-05-20%2Bat%2B10.00.34.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"><img data-original-height=\"503\" data-original-width=\"1600\" height=\"198\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ZkvwVqhZu00/Xuyh83uAZ6I/AAAAAAAABOQ/veJ_KXh8mFEB2uxPp_H82FwdQlTVlN6bgCK4BGAsYHg/w625-h198/Screenshot%2B2020-05-20%2Bat%2B10.00.34.png\" style=\"border: solid black;\" width=\"625\" /></a></td>\n   </tr>\n   <tr>\n    <td class=\"tr-caption\" style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 9pt; font-style: italic; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Out with the old, in with the new; some of the form controls refresh that landed in Chrome 83. (</span><a href=\"https://blog.chromium.org/2020/03/updates-to-form-controls-and-focus.html\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 9pt; font-style: italic; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">more in the blogpost</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 9pt; font-style: italic; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">).</span><br /></td>\n   </tr>\n  </tbody>\n </table><p></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">In terms of behavior, there appears to be a general concern that form control behaviors either aren't well specified or that those specifications aren't consistently followed by browsers. Some concrete examples of inconsistencies across browsers that we heard are support for certain &lt;input&gt; types, autofill behaviors, and content restoration behavior when navigating away from and back to pages that contain forms. Again we have nothing specific to announce yet, but will be looking at this area going forward.</span></p><h2 dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 6pt; margin-top: 18pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 16pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">CSS Grid</span></h2><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Like Flexbox, </span><a href=\"https://web.dev/responsive-web-design-basics/#grid\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">CSS Grid</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> is an important component of modern layout. Looking at the early survey results it seems like the story for CSS Grid support in Chromium is fairly good (we have our friends from </span><a href=\"https://www.igalia.com/\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Igalia</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> to thank for that!). There is one clear exception - Chromium still doesn't support </span><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/CSS_Grid_Layout/Subgrid\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">subgrid</span></a><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">.</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Hopefully it won't be an exception for much longer. It's still early days, but I'm excited to share that a team at Microsoft Edge are working on rearchitecting Chromium's Grid support to use the new LayoutNG engine - and as part of this are intending to add subgrid support! We're excited to see this feature land and want to express our appreciation to our partners at Microsoft, Igalia, and the many other Chromium contributors who have worked on CSS Grid support.</span></p><h2 dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 6pt; margin-top: 18pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 16pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Launching features on the web</span></h2><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Unlike many platforms, the web has multiple implementations. This has downsides but it is also one of the web's greatest strengths. It vastly widens the diversity of inputs into the web platform, and provides a guarding factor against architectural mistakes that can occur when one blurs a platform (the web) and an implementation (a single browser).</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">In Chrome we strongly believe in moving the web forward, and in shipping new features that bring benefits to users and developers. But it is clear from the MDN Browser Compatibility Survey that some developers have concerns about how this may impact compatibility. We aren't going to stop moving the web forward, but we are planning to be more rigorous in how we approach it and in how we communicate about compatibility.&nbsp; Look out for more on this soon.</span></p><h2 dir=\"ltr\" id=\"summing-up\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 6pt; margin-top: 18pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 16pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Summing up</span></h2><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">When it comes to browser compatibility, there are still too many missing features and edge-case bugs. But it doesn't have to be this way. Things can and will get better, if browser vendors can understand what is causing the most pain, and take action to address the causes. In Chrome we're doing our best to listen, and we're doing our best to address what we're hearing. We hope it helps, and we're looking forward to a more compatible 2021.</span></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"><br /></span></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">For all of the above, <b>please tell us if we're right or wrong</b>. <a href=\"https://twitter.com/ChromiumDev\" target=\"_blank\">Tweet us</a>, <a href=\"https://crbug.com\" target=\"_blank\">file bugs</a> and star the issues that you think we should prioritize, fill in <a href=\"https://forms.gle/oa1h7xsJPobaodobA\" target=\"_blank\">this form</a>, take part in the next web survey you see. Your voice matters to us and is a major factor in determining what work we prioritize.</span></p><br /></span>\n<div>\n <span><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"><br /></span></span>\n</div>\n<div>\n <span><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"><br /></span></span>\n</div>\n<div>\n <span><span style=\"font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Posted by Stephen McGruer, Software Engineer, Chrome</span></span>\n</div>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Thu, 18 Jun 2020 14:28:00 +0000","feedId":649,"bgimg":"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8TebBC73ZJI/Xuyhb3lkHkI/AAAAAAAABN8/aa0ROlMNtXgxAE5BOeGuUg4PjBc7qkYpwCK4BGAsYHg/w625-h193/Screenshot%2B2020-05-15%2Bat%2B09.23.59.jpg","linkMd5":"2cbdc6f62510d1b80d9ef6b57695485b","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn26@2020_4/2020/08/16/12-29-50-056_4448db3e02c790da.webp","destWidth":625,"destHeight":192,"author":"Chromium Blog","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8TebBC73ZJI/Xuyhb3lkHkI/AAAAAAAABN8/aa0ROlMNtXgxAE5BOeGuUg4PjBc7qkYpwCK4BGAsYHg/w625-h193/Screenshot%2B2020-05-15%2Bat%2B09.23.59.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn2@2020_1/2020/08/16/12-29-50-181_4448db3e02c790da.webp","https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ZkvwVqhZu00/Xuyh83uAZ6I/AAAAAAAABOQ/veJ_KXh8mFEB2uxPp_H82FwdQlTVlN6bgCK4BGAsYHg/w625-h198/Screenshot%2B2020-05-20%2Bat%2B10.00.34.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn65@2020_5/2020/08/16/12-29-50-193_c3930934f37d1d39.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-16 20:29:49","updatedTime":"2020-08-16 20:29:49","title":"Changes to quality criteria for PWAs using Trusted Web Activity","link":"http://blog.chromium.org/2020/06/changes-to-quality-criteria-for-pwas.html","description":"<span id=\"docs-internal-guid-95c75256-7fff-4a74-cb56-68e481107423\"><span style=\"color: #666666; font-family: Arial; font-size: 15pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Trusted Web Activity will delegate some web app errors to native app crashes beginning in Chrome 86</span></span><div><span><span style=\"color: #666666; font-family: Arial; font-size: 15pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"><br /></span></span></div><div><span id=\"docs-internal-guid-cc0a2042-7fff-8c99-7812-ef6c918fb7de\"><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><a href=\"https://developers.google.com/web/android/trusted-web-activity\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Trusted Web Activities</span></a><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> are Chrome's recommended way to integrate fullscreen Progressive Web App content into an Android app. Unlike a WebView, a Trusted Web Activity is an instance of the Chrome browser and implements a complete and evergreen set of web platform APIs thanks to Chrome auto update. Since the release of Trusted Web Activity, we’ve been working on improving the integration of apps built using a Trusted Web Activity into the native ecosystem with features such as automatically generated splash screens and web notification delegation.&nbsp;</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">In Chrome 86, we’ll take this integration a step further by delegating web application crash events into native equivalents.&nbsp;</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Web apps crash, but they crash differently</span></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Web developers are more used to thinking about “errors” rather than crashes. When a user encounters an HTTP error in their web app journey, such as a 404 or a 5xx error, that’s effectively an application crash. Another example of a web app error that could be considered a crash is when the Chrome dino page appears because the user lost their internet connection and the app didn’t have a handler in the ServiceWorker for an offline resource request. This kind of ServiceWorker handling of errors can be used for 404 and 5xx resource loading errors as well.&nbsp;</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Crashes in the Android ecosystem</span></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><a href=\"https://developer.android.com/topic/performance/vitals\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Android Vitals</span></a><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> is an initiative by Google to improve the stability and performance of Android devices. The Google Play </span><a href=\"https://play.google.com/console/about/\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Console</span></a><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> aggregates Android Vitals data and displays it in the Android vitals </span><a href=\"https://support.google.com/googleplay/android-developer/answer/7385505\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">dashboard</span></a><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">. Problems in Android Vitals indicate a low quality user experience in the app and can result in bad ratings and poor discoverability on the Play Store.</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Starting in Chrome 86, Chrome will integrate critical web application crashes into native app crash events and Android Vitals. As this change will cause user facing crashes if these events are unhandled, developers using or planning to use a Trusted Web Activity should review this post carefully.</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Critical web application crashes that will be delegated in Chrome 86 are:&nbsp;</span></p><br /><ol style=\"margin-bottom: 0; margin-top: 0;\"><li dir=\"ltr\" style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\"><p dir=\"ltr\" role=\"presentation\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">an HTTP 404 or 5xx error in the application</span></p></li><li dir=\"ltr\" style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\"><p dir=\"ltr\" role=\"presentation\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">failure to return HTTP 200 for an offline network resource request</span></p></li><li dir=\"ltr\" style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\"><p dir=\"ltr\" role=\"presentation\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">failure to verify digital asset links at application launch</span></p></li></ol><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">In this article we’ll provide more details on the exception conditions, impact on the application behavior and how to avoid these exceptions.&nbsp;</span></p><h1 dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 6pt; margin-top: 20pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 20pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Why is Chrome making this change?</span></h1><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Users installing an Android application from the Play Store expect the application to look and feel native. Native applications do not have a 404 or 5xx error page. Native applications are expected to handle internet service interruptions, at a minimum by providing a branded offline indicator. Finally, when digital asset links fail to verify, we cannot verify that the app owner is also the owner of the web content. Previously, this circumstance resulted in a fallback from Trusted web Activity to a CCT view. In practice we’ve found that a CCT fallback does not meet user expectations. Furthermore, the silent fallback bypasses a feedback mechanism (a Play console crash report) that is important for developers to understand what’s going wrong with their application.&nbsp;</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">By integrating crash events into Android Vitals, Android app developers using Trusted Web Activity can make use of the Android Vitals </span><a href=\"https://support.google.com/googleplay/android-developer/answer/7385505\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; text-decoration-line: underline; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">dashboard</span></a><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> to view information about the user experience of their app. This approach also rewards developers building high quality apps, since apps with better scores in Android vitals have better discoverability in the Play store.&nbsp;</span></p><h1 dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 6pt; margin-top: 20pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 20pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">How will this work and what should I do about it?&nbsp;</span></h1><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">The table below details the web application crash triggers, the corresponding action and recommended mitigations. However, consider avoiding these exceptions altogether with the mitigations recommended in the table above.&nbsp;</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">First, the Trusted Web Activity exception will cause Chrome to exit. Even if the&nbsp; exception is handled, it will still be a janky user experience.&nbsp;</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Second, implementing the mitigations in the web app will improve the experience of all users of your PWA in all web browsers.&nbsp;</span></p><h1 dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Over time, we will continue to add integrations of important web application events into Android Vitals to make the user experience of web applications more consistent with native applications.&nbsp;</span></p><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; Android apps using Trusted Web Activity must comply with all Play store policies, including for web content in the Trusted Web Activity, including policies for payments in-app purchases and other digital goods.&nbsp;</span></p></li><li dir=\"ltr\" style=\"font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\"><p dir=\"ltr\" role=\"presentation\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">To ensure the quality of experience, content in a Trusted Web Activity must meet PWA installability criteria and load fast at the start URL. pre-wrap;\">Lighthouse</span></a><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> at the Trusted Web Activity start URL and must achieve a performance score of 80.&nbsp;</span></p></li></ol><br /><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><a href=\"https://developers.google.com/web/tools/lighthouse/\" style=\"text-decoration-line: none;\"><span style=\"color: #1155cc; font-family: Arial; font-size: 11pt; font-variant-east-asian: normal; progressive web apps and is useful both as a benchmark and to help you build better websites.&nbsp;</span></p><h1 dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 6pt; margin-top: 20pt;
